9-32 Decklists
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 21, 2017 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20170709072651im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/themes/wiz_mtg/images/global/generic-avatar-150.png)
By Meghan Wolff and Marc Calderaro











Just because the Top 8 hogs the spotlight, doesn't mean the deck delights stop there. Check out what the rest of the Top 32 finishers played at Grand Prix Montreal!
